       509    
       510 -  **Last Updated:** November 15, 2025
       510 +  ## Checkpoint Automation System
       511 +  
       512 +  ### Overview
       513 +  
       514 +  CODITECT includes an automated checkpoint creation system that:
       515 +  - ‚úÖ Standardizes checkpoint format (ISO-DATETIME stamped)
       516 +  - ‚úÖ Captures git status, submodule states, completed tasks
       517 +  - ‚úÖ Updates README.md with checkpoint reference
       518 +  - ‚úÖ Creates MEMORY-CONTEXT session export
       519 +  - ‚úÖ Enables zero catastrophic forgetting between sessions
       520 +  - ‚úÖ Saves tokens through reusable checkpoint template
       521 +  
       522 +  ### When to Create Checkpoints
       523 +  
       524 +  Create checkpoints after:
       525 +  - Completing a sprint (Phase 0, Sprint +1, Sprint +2, etc.)
       526 +  - Major architectural changes
       527 +  - Completing multiple submodule updates
       528 +  - Finishing documentation sprints
       529 +  - Phase gate completions
       530 +  - End of development session (for context continuity)
       531 +  
       532 +  ### How to Create Checkpoints
       533 +  
       534 +  **Single Command:**
       535 +  ```bash
       536 +  python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "Sprint description" --auto-commit
       537 +  ```
       538 +  
       539 +  **Examples:**
       540 +  ```bash
       541 +  # After architecture sprint
       542 +  python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "Architecture Documentation Sprint Complete" 
           + --auto-commit
       543 +  
       544 +  # After MEMORY-CONTEXT implementation
       545 +  python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "Sprint +1 MEMORY-CONTEXT Implementation Complete" 
           + --auto-commit
       546 +  
       547 +  # After updating TASKLISTs
       548 +  python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "TASKLISTs Updated Across All Submodules" 
           + --auto-commit
       549 +  
       550 +  # Manual commit (without --auto-commit)
       551 +  python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "Sprint description"
       552 +  # Then manually review and commit
       553 +  ```
       554 +  
       555 +  ### What the Script Does
       556 +  
       557 +  1. **Generates Checkpoint Document** (`CHECKPOINTS/YYYY-MM-DDTHH-MM-SSZ-description.md`)
       558 +     - Git status and recent commits
       559 +     - Submodule status and latest commits
       560 +     - Completed tasks from all TASKLISTs
       561 +     - Changed files summary
       562 +     - Next steps and Sprint +1 preparation
       563 +  
       564 +  2. **Updates README.md**
       565 +     - Adds checkpoint to "Recent Checkpoints" section
       566 +     - Links to checkpoint document
       567 +     - Maintains chronological order
       568 +  
       569 +  3. **Creates MEMORY-CONTEXT Export** 
           + (`MEMORY-CONTEXT/sessions/YYYY-MM-DD-description.md`)
       570 +     - Session summary
       571 +     - Objectives completed
       572 +     - Key decisions
       573 +     - Work completed reference
       574 +     - Next session preparation
       575 +  
       576 +  4. **Commits Changes** (if --auto-commit flag used)
       577 +     - Commits checkpoint, README.md, and MEMORY-CONTEXT export
       578 +     - Standardized commit message with metadata
       579 +  
       580 +  ### Benefits for AI Agents
       581 +  
       582 +  **Context Continuity:**
       583 +  - Next session starts with complete checkpoint context
       584 +  - Zero catastrophic forgetting via MEMORY-CONTEXT export
       585 +  - Clear understanding of what was completed
       586 +  
       587 +  **Token Efficiency:**
       588 +  - Reusable checkpoint template (don't recreate format each time)
       589 +  - Standardized structure saves tokens
       590 +  - Links to detailed TASKLISTs instead of duplicating
       591 +  
       592 +  **Informed Decision Making:**
       593 +  - Historical checkpoints show progression
       594 +  - Pattern recognition across sprints
       595 +  - Dependencies and blockers tracked
       596 +  
       597 +  ### Claude Code Integration
       598 +  
       599 +  When working in this repository:
       600 +  
       601 +  1. **Start of Session:** Read most recent checkpoint
       602 +     ```bash
       603 +     # Find most recent checkpoint
       604 +     ls -t CHECKPOINTS/ | head -1
       605 +     ```
       606 +  
       607 +  2. **During Work:** Track progress in TASKLISTs
       608 +     - Mark completed tasks with `[x]`
       609 +     - Add new tasks as discovered
       610 +     - Update WIP status
       611 +  
       612 +  3. **End of Session:** Create checkpoint
       613 +     ```bash
       614 +     python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py "Session description" --auto-commit
       615 +     ```
       616 +  
       617 +  4. **Next Session:** Load checkpoint context
       618 +     - Read most recent checkpoint document
       619 +     - Review MEMORY-CONTEXT session export
       620 +     - Continue from where previous session ended
       621 +  
       622 +  ### Script Location and Documentation
       623 +  
       624 +  - **Script:** `scripts/create-checkpoint.py`
       625 +  - **Documentation:** See script header for detailed usage
       626 +  - **Help:** `python3 scripts/create-checkpoint.py --help`
       627 +

  ‚úÖ Export Automation System Complete

  Files Created

  1. scripts/export-context.sh - Main automation script
  - Generates ISO-DATETIME timestamps (YYYY-MM-DDTHH-MM-SSZ)
  - Creates export directory (MEMORY-CONTEXT/exports/)
  - Generates standardized filename with description
  - Creates placeholder file with instructions
  - Creates symlink to latest-export.txt
  - Provides git commit instructions
  - Returns filepath for scripting

  2. commands/export - Simple wrapper command
  - Easy-to-use shortcut: ./commands/export [description]
  - Passes arguments to main script

  3. docs/EXPORT-AUTOMATION.md - Comprehensive documentation
  - Quick start guide
  - Detailed usage instructions
  - Integration with MEMORY-CONTEXT system
  - Best practices
  - Troubleshooting
  - Use cases and examples

  How to Use

  From any CODITECT project:

  # Simple export
  .coditect/scripts/export-context.sh

  # With description
  .coditect/scripts/export-context.sh "Sprint Planning Complete"

  What happens:

  1. Script generates ISO-DATETIME timestamp
  2. Creates filename: 2025-11-16T10-45-32Z-Sprint-Planning-Complete.txt
  3. Creates directory: MEMORY-CONTEXT/exports/
  4. Creates placeholder file
  5. Shows instructions for /export command
  6. Creates symlink: latest-export.txt ‚Üí newest export
  7. Provides git commit commands

  Then you:

  1. Run /export in Claude Code
  2. Paste the provided filepath
  3. Export completes automatically
  4. Commit to git (optional)

  ‚úÖ Available to all 19 submodules via .coditect symlink
  ‚úÖ Consistent naming across all projects
  ‚úÖ Unified storage in MEMORY-CONTEXT/exports/
  ‚úÖ Cross-project patterns via NESTED LEARNING
  ‚úÖ Privacy-controlled exports

‚è∫ Here are my comprehensive suggestions for the unified workflow:

  1. Command Hierarchy (Simple ‚Üí Advanced)

  Simple Commands:
  export              # Quick: Just export session context
  checkpoint          # Full: Export ‚Üí checkpoint ‚Üí commit ‚Üí push

  Advanced Options:
  checkpoint --no-push         # Skip GitHub push
  checkpoint --skip-export     # Just checkpoint (already have export)
  checkpoint --description "..." # Custom description

  2. Directory Structure (Consolidation)

  YES - Consolidate into MEMORY-CONTEXT:
  MEMORY-CONTEXT/
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ checkpoints/     # ‚Üê Move CHECKPOINTS/ here
  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ sessions/        # Processed session context
  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ exports/         # Raw export files (.txt from /export)

  Benefits:
  - Single source of truth for session continuity
  - Easier backup/sync
  - Cleaner root directory
  - Logical grouping

  3. Unified Script Architecture

  Create: scripts/checkpoint-session.py (Master orchestrator)

  Calls in sequence:
  1. session_export.py - Extract from checkpoint
  2. Create checkpoint document
  3. Update README.md (current repo)
  4. Git operations (add, commit)
  5. If submodule: Update master README.md + submodule pointer
  6. Push all affected repos

  4. README.md Update Strategy

  Automatic section management:
  ## Recent Checkpoints

  - **[2025-11-16](MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints/2025-11-16T13-17-06Z-description.md)** - Description
  - [2025-11-15](MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints/...) - Previous
  (Keep last 5-10, archive older ones)

  5. Git Workflow

  In current repo:
  git add MEMORY-CONTEXT/ README.md
  git commit -m "Checkpoint: Description

  - Session: MEMORY-CONTEXT/sessions/...
  - Checkpoint: MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints/...

  ü§ñ Claude Code | Co-Authored-By: Claude"
  git push

  In master (if submodule):
  cd ../../  # Navigate to master
  git add submodules/coditect-project-dot-claude README.md
  git commit -m "Update framework: Checkpoint created"
  git push

  6. Migration Strategy

  Phase 1: Move CHECKPOINTS/
  mv CHECKPOINTS/* MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints/
  rmdir CHECKPOINTS
  git mv CHECKPOINTS MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints  # Preserve history

  Phase 2: Update Scripts
  - Update all references to CHECKPOINTS/ ‚Üí MEMORY-CONTEXT/checkpoints/
  - Update create-checkpoint.py
  - Test all workflows

  Phase 3: Deploy Unified Script
  - Create checkpoint-session.py
  - Test end-to-end
  - Update documentation

  7. Error Handling & Safety

  # Checks before operations
  - Verify in git repo
  - Check for uncommitted changes (warn user)
  - Validate submodule structure
  - Confirm push permissions
  - Rollback on failure

  # User prompts
  - "Push to GitHub? [Y/n]"
  - "Update master repo? [Y/n]" (if submodule)

  8. Configuration File (Optional)

  .coditect/checkpoint.config.json:
  {
    "auto_export": true,
    "auto_commit": true,
    "auto_push": true,
    "update_readme": true,
    "update_master_if_submodule": true,
    "keep_recent_checkpoints": 10
  }

  9. Backward Compatibility

  Keep existing scripts working:
  - export-context.sh ‚Üí calls new system
  - create-checkpoint.py ‚Üí wrapper to unified script
  - session_export.py ‚Üí still works standalone

  Gradual migration path for users
